                    <div class="tab-content">
                        <div role="tabpanel" class="tab-pane fade" id="tab-description">
                            <div class="desc-text" itemprop="description">
                                The Regressed Mercenary’s Machinations Light Novel
A Rogue Guard in a Medieval Fantasy Novel,
Roguish Guard in a Medieval Fantasy Novel,
The Chaotic Guard Captain in a Fantasy World Novel,
The Rogue Captain of the Guards in a Medieval Fantasy World Novel,
중세 판타지 속 망나니 경비조장
Description: 
One of the seven strongest people on the continent, the King of Mercenaries.
He started a war to avenge his fallen family and destroyed territory but failed and lost his life.
However…
“Wow, I’m alive?”
I returned to the past, back through time.
A perfect opportunity to right my regrets and reverse everything.
It doesn’t matter if people around me point fingers, calling me a scoundrel, or dismiss me as tr*sh.
Because…
“I’ve got a plan.”
“What plan?”
“A plan to destroy everything.”
There won’t be a second failure.
This time, I’ll wipe out all my enemies.
…But first, I need to rebuild this damn estate.
                            </div>

                        </div>

                            <script>
                                let skip = 0; 
                                let sortOrder = 'latest'; 
                            
                                const limit = 10; 
                            
                                let isLoading = false; 
                            
                            
                            
                                async function showNovelComment() {
                                    const commentContainer = document.getElementById('novel-comment');
                                    const loadMoreButton = document.getElementById('load-more-comments');
                            
                                    // if (commentContainer.innerHTML.trim() !== '') {
                                    // commentContainer.style.display = "block";
                            
                                    //return;
                                    //}
                                    const loadingMessage = document.getElementById('loading-message');
                                    loadingMessage.style.display = 'block';
                            
                                    try {
                                        const response = await fetch(`/ajax/comments?skip=0&novel_id=the-regressed-mercenarys-machinations&sort=${sortOrder}`); 
                            
                                        if (response.ok) {
                                            const html = await response.text();
                                            const commentHeaderCount = (html.match(/main-comment /g) || []).length;
                            
                                            commentContainer.innerHTML = html;
                                            if (html.trim() == '' || commentHeaderCount < 10) {
                                                loadMoreButton.style.display = "none";
                                            } else {
                                                loadMoreButton.style.display = "block";
                                            }
                                            commentContainer.style.display = "block";
                                        } else {
                                            console.error('Failed to load comments:', response.status);
                                            commentContainer.innerHTML = `<p>Error loading comments. Please try again later.</p>`;
                                            commentContainer.style.display = "block";
                                        }
                                    } catch (error) {
                                        console.error('Error fetching comments:', error);
                                        commentContainer.innerHTML = `<p>Error loading comments. Please try again later.</p>`;
                                        commentContainer.style.display = "block";
                                    } finally {
                                        loadingMessage.style.display = 'none';
                                    }
                                }
                            
                                async function loadMoreComments() {
                                    const commentContainer = document.getElementById('novel-comment');
                                    const loadMoreButton = document.getElementById('load-more-comments');
                            
                                    if (isLoading) return;
                                    isLoading = true;
                            
                                    loadMoreButton.disabled = true;
                                    loadMoreButton.innerText = "Loading..."; 
                                    skip += limit; 
                            
                                    try {
                                        const response = await fetch(`/ajax/comments?skip=${skip}&novel_id=the-regressed-mercenarys-machinations&sort=${sortOrder}`);
                            
                                        if (response.ok) {
                                            const html = await response.text();
                            
                                            commentContainer.innerHTML += html;
                            
                                            if (html.trim() === '') {
                                                loadMoreButton.style.display = "none";
                                            }
                                        } else {
                                            console.error('Failed to load more comments:', response.status);
                                        }
                                    } catch (error) {
                                        console.error('Error loading more comments:', error);
                                    } finally {
                                        isLoading = false;
                                        loadMoreButton.disabled = false;
                                        loadMoreButton.innerText = "Load More"; 
                                    }
                                }
                            
                                function updateSortAndReloadComments() {
                                    const sortSelect = document.getElementById('sort-comments');
                                    sortOrder = sortSelect.value;
                                    console.log(sortOrder)
                                    skip = 0;
                            
                                    showNovelComment();
                                }
                            
                            </script>
                            
                            
                            <script>
                                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
                              
                            
                                    function isUserLoggedIn() {
                                        return !!document.querySelector('.glyphicon.glyphicon-log-out');
                                    }
                            
                                    document.addEventListener('click', async (event) => {
                                        if (event.target.classList.contains('glyphicon-thumbs-up')) {
                            
                                            if (!isUserLoggedIn()) {
                                                window.location.href = '/login-types';
                                                return;
                                            }
                            
                                            const button = event.target;
                                            const commentId = button.getAttribute('data-id');
                            
                                            const requestBody = { _csrf: csrf }; 
                            
                                            try {
                                                const response = await fetch(`/comments/${commentId}/like`, {
                                                    method: 'POST',
                                                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                                                    body: JSON.stringify(requestBody),
                                                });
                            
                                                if (response.ok) {
                                                    const data = await response.json();
                            
                                                    const likeCountElement = button.closest('.comment-footer').querySelector('.like-count');
                                                    if (likeCountElement) {
                                                        likeCountElement.textContent = data.likes; 
                                                    }
                            
                                                    const dislikeCountElement = button.closest('.comment-footer').querySelector('.dislike-count');
                                                    if (dislikeCountElement) {
                                                        dislikeCountElement.textContent = data.dislikes; 
                                                    }
                                                    button.classList.add('liked');
                                                    const dislikeButton = button.closest('.comment-footer').querySelector('.glyphicon-thumbs-down');
                                                    if (dislikeButton) {
                                                        dislikeButton.classList.remove('disliked');
                                                    }
                                                } else {
                                                    console.error('Failed to like the comment');
                                                }
                                            } catch (error) {
                                                console.error('Error liking the comment:', error);
                                            }
                                        }
                                    });
                            
                                    document.addEventListener('click', async (event) => {
                                        if (event.target.classList.contains('glyphicon-thumbs-down')) {
                                            console.log("Dislike button clicked");
                            
                                            if (!isUserLoggedIn()) {
                                                window.location.href = 'https://novelbin.com/login-types';
                                                return;
                                            }
                            
                                            const button = event.target;
                                            const commentId = button.getAttribute('data-id');
                            
                                            const requestBody = { _csrf: csrf }; 
                            
                                            try {
                                                const response = await fetch(`/comments/${commentId}/dislike`, {
                                                    method: 'POST',
                                                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                                                    body: JSON.stringify(requestBody),
                                                });
                            
                                                if (response.ok) {
                                                    const data = await response.json();
                            
                                                    const likeCountElement = button.closest('.comment-footer').querySelector('.like-count');
                                                    if (likeCountElement) {
                                                        likeCountElement.textContent = data.likes; 
                                                    }
                            
                                                    const dislikeCountElement = button.closest('.comment-footer').querySelector('.dislike-count');
                                                    if (dislikeCountElement) {
                                                        dislikeCountElement.textContent = data.dislikes; 
                                                    }
                            
                                                    button.classList.add('disliked');
                                                    const likeButton = button.closest('.comment-footer').querySelector('.glyphicon-thumbs-up');
                                                    if (likeButton) {
                                                        likeButton.classList.remove('liked');
                                                    }
                                                } else {
                                                    console.error('Failed to dislike the comment');
                                                }
                                            } catch (error) {
                                                console.error('Error disliking the comment:', error);
                                            }
                                        }
                                    });
                                });
                            </script>

                            <script>
                                document.getElementById('submit-comment').addEventListener('click', async () => {
                                    const content = tinymce.get('editor-container').getContent();
                                    const novel_id = "the-regressed-mercenarys-machinations";
                                    const chapterInfo = "" ? { title: "", url: 'https://novelbin.com/b//' } : null;
                                    let isLoading = false;
                                    function isUserLoggedIn() {
                                        return !!document.querySelector('.glyphicon.glyphicon-log-out');
                                    }
                            
                                    if (!isUserLoggedIn()) {
                                        window.location.href = '/login-types';
                                        return;
                                    }
                            
                            
                                    if (!content) {
                                        alert('Comment cannot be empty');
                                        return;
                                    }
                                    const postCommentButton = document.getElementById('submit-comment');
                                    try {
                            
                            
                            
                                        if (isLoading) return;
                                        isLoading = true;
                                        postCommentButton.disabled = true;
                                        postCommentButton.innerText = "Loading..."; 
                                        const response = await fetch('/comments', {
                                            method: 'POST',
                                            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                                            body: JSON.stringify({ content, novel_id, chapter: chapterInfo, _csrf: csrf })
                                        });
                            
                                        if (response.ok) {
                                            const html = await response.text();
                                            const commentContainer = document.getElementById('novel-comment');
                                            commentContainer.insertAdjacentHTML('afterbegin', html);
                                        } else {
                            
                                            if (response.status === 429) {
                                                const data = await response.json();
                                                alert(data.message); 
                                                return;
                                            }
                            
                            
                                            alert("Failed to post comment");
                                        }
                                    } catch (error) {
                                        console.error('Error posting comment:', error);
                                        alert('Failed to post comment');
                                    } finally {
                                        isLoading = false;
                                        postCommentButton.disabled = false;
                                        postCommentButton.innerText = "Post Comment"; 
                                    }
                                });
                            </script>

                            <div id="reply-popup" class="reply-popup" style="display: none;">
                                <div class="popup-content">
                                    <span class="close-popup">×</span>
                                    <h4>Reply to <span id="reply-username"></span></h4>
                                    <textarea style="margin-top: 15px;" id="reply-content" class="form-control" rows="4" placeholder="Write your reply here..."></textarea>
                                    <button style="margin-top: 15px;" class="btn btn-default btn-sm" id="submit-reply">Submit Reply</button>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            
                            
                            <script>
                            
                                function isUserLoggedIn() {
                                    return !!document.querySelector('.glyphicon.glyphicon-log-out');
                                }
                                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
                                    const replyPopup = document.getElementById('reply-popup');
                                    const replyContent = document.getElementById('reply-content');
                                    const replyUsername = document.getElementById('reply-username');
                                    const submitReplyButton = document.getElementById('submit-reply');
                            
                                    let parentCommentId = null;
                            
                                    document.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
                                        if (event.target.classList.contains('btn-reply')) {
                                            event.preventDefault();
                            
                                            if (!isUserLoggedIn()) {
                                                window.location.href = '/login-types';
                                                return;
                                            }
                            
                                            parentCommentId = event.target.getAttribute('data-id');
                                            const username = event.target.getAttribute('data-username');
                            
                                            replyUsername.textContent = username;
                            
                                            replyPopup.style.display = 'flex';
                                        }
                                    });
                            
                                    document.querySelector('.close-popup').addEventListener('click', () => {
                                        replyPopup.style.display = 'none';
                                        replyContent.value = ''; 
                                    });
                            
                                    submitReplyButton.addEventListener('click', async () => {
                                        const content = replyContent.value.trim();
                            
                                        if (!content) {
                                            alert('Please enter your reply content.');
                                            return;
                                        }
                            
                                        try {
                                            submitReplyButton.innerText = 'Loading...';
                                            submitReplyButton.disabled = true;
                            
                                            const response = await fetch('/comments', {
                                                method: 'POST',
                                                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                                                body: JSON.stringify({
                                                    content: content,
                                                    parent_comment: parentCommentId,
                                                    novel_id: "the-regressed-mercenarys-machinations",
                                                    _csrf: csrf
                                                })
                                            });
                            
                                            if (response.ok) {
                            
                            
                            
                                                const html = await response.text(); 
                                                const parentComment = document.querySelector(`.comment[data-id="${parentCommentId}"]`);
                            
                                                if (parentComment) {
                                                    const nestedComments = parentComment.querySelector('.nested-comments');
                            
                                                    if (nestedComments) {
                                                        parentComment.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', `<div class = "nested-comments">${html}</div>`);
                                                    } else {
                                                        const newNestedContainer = document.createElement('div');
                                                        newNestedContainer.classList.add('nested-comments');
                                                        newNestedContainer.innerHTML = html;
                                                        parentComment.appendChild(newNestedContainer);
                                                    }
                                                } else {
                                                    console.error('Parent comment not found');
                                                }
                                            } else {
                            
                                                if (response.status === 429) {
                                                    const data = await response.json();
                                                    alert(data.message); 
                                                    return;
                                                }
                            
                            
                                                alert('Failed to submit reply.');
                                            }
                                        } catch (error) {
                                            console.error('Error submitting reply:', error);
                                            alert('Failed to submit reply.');
                                        } finally {
                                            replyPopup.style.display = 'none';
                                            replyContent.value = ''; 
                            
                                            submitReplyButton.innerText = 'Submit Reply';
                                            submitReplyButton.disabled = false;
                                        }
                                    });
                                });
                            </script>
                            
                            
                            <script>
                                document.addEventListener('click', async (event) => {
                                    if (event.target.classList.contains('btn-delete')) {
                                        event.preventDefault();
                            
                                        const commentId = event.target.getAttribute('data-id');
                            
                                        if (!confirm('Are you sure you want to delete this comment?')) return;
                            
                                        try {
                                            const response = await fetch(`/api/comments/${commentId}`, {
                                                method: 'DELETE',
                                                headers: {
                                                    'Content-Type': 'application/json'
                                                },
                                                body: JSON.stringify({
                                                    _csrf: csrf
                                                })
                                            });
                            
                                            if (response.ok) {
                                                const commentElement = document.querySelector(`.comment[data-id="${commentId}"]`);
                                                if (commentElement) commentElement.remove();
                            
                                                alert('Comment deleted successfully.');
                                            } else {
                                                const error = await response.json();
                                                alert(`Failed to delete comment: ${error.message}`);
                                            }
                                        } catch (error) {
                                            console.error('Error deleting comment:', error);
                                            alert('An error occurred while deleting the comment.');
                                        }
                                    }
                                });
                            
                            </script>
                            
                            <script>
                                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
                            
                                    tinymce.init({
                                        selector: '#editor-container',
                                        content_css: 'https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/tinymce-all-in-one@4.9.5/skins/lightgray/content.min.css',
                                        plugins: 'link lists table',
                                        toolbar: 'bold italic underline | emoji | bullist numlist | link', 
                                        menubar: false,
                                        branding: false,
                                        setup: function (editor) {
                                            editor.addButton('emoji', {
                                                text: '😊', 
                                                type: 'menubutton',
                                                icon: false,
                                                menu: [
                                                    { text: '😊 Smile', onclick: function () { editor.insertContent('😊'); } },
                                                    { text: '🔥 Fire', onclick: function () { editor.insertContent('🔥'); } },
                                                    { text: '❤️ Heart', onclick: function () { editor.insertContent('❤️'); } },
                                                    { text: '🎉 Party', onclick: function () { editor.insertContent('🎉'); } },
                                                    { text: '📖 Book', onclick: function () { editor.insertContent('📖'); } },
                                                    { text: '✍️ Writing', onclick: function () { editor.insertContent('✍️'); } },

                            <script>
                            
                                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {
                                    const novelId = "the-regressed-mercenarys-machinations"; 
                                    const reactionsContainer = document.getElementById('reactions');
                            
                                    try {
                                        const response = await fetch('/api/init-reactions/the-regressed-mercenarys-machinations', {
                                            method: 'GET',
                                            headers: {
                                                'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                                            }
                                        });
                            
                                        if (response.ok) {
                                            const data = await response.json();
                                            // Highlight user reaction
                                            if (data.userReaction) {
                                                const reactionElement = document.querySelector(`.reaction[data-reaction="${data.userReaction}"]`);
                                                if (reactionElement) {
                                                    reactionElement.classList.add('highlight');
                                                }
                                            }
                                            updateReactionCounts(data.reactions);
                            
                                   
                            
                                        } else {
                                            const errorData = await response.json();
                                            console.error('Error initializing reactions:', errorData.message);
                                        }
                                    } catch (error) {
                                        console.error('Failed to initialize reactions:', error);
                                    }finally{
                                         reactionsContainer.style.display = 'block';
                                    }
                                });
                            
                                function updateReactionCounts(reactionCounts) {
                                    for (const [reactionType, count] of Object.entries(reactionCounts)) {
                                        const countElement = document.getElementById(`${reactionType}-count`);
                                        if (countElement) {
                                            countElement.textContent = count; 
                                        }
                                    }
                            
                                    const totalResponsesElement = document.getElementById('total-responses');
                                    if (totalResponsesElement) {
                                        const totalResponses = Object.values(reactionCounts).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
                                        totalResponsesElement.textContent = totalResponses;
                                    }
                                }
                            
                                document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
                                    const reactionButtons = document.querySelectorAll(".reaction");
                            
                                    reactionButtons.forEach((button) => {
                                        button.addEventListener("click", async () => {
                            
                                            if (!isUserLoggedIn()) {
                                                window.location.href = '/login-types';
                                                return;
                                            }
                            
                            
                                            const reactionType = button.getAttribute("data-reaction");
                            
                                            const novel_id = "the-regressed-mercenarys-machinations"; 
                            
                                            try {
                                                const response = await fetch("/api/reaction", {
                                                    method: "POST",
                                                    headers: {
                                                        "Content-Type": "application/json",
                                                    },
                                                    body: JSON.stringify({
                                                        novel_id,
                                                        reaction: reactionType,
                                                        _csrf: csrf
                                                    }),
                                                });
                            
                                                if (!response.ok) {
                                                    const errorData = await response.json();
                                                    console.error("API Error:", errorData);
                                                    return;
                                                }
                            
                                                const data = await response.json();
                            
                                                const reactionCounts = data.reactions; 
                                                updateReactionCounts(reactionCounts);
                            
                                                // Remove the 'highlight' class from all reaction buttons
                                                reactionButtons.forEach((btn) => btn.classList.remove('highlight'));
                            
                                                // Add the 'highlight' class to the clicked button
                                                button.classList.add('highlight');
                            
                            
                                            } catch (error) {
                                                console.error("Failed to update reaction:", error);
                                            }
                                        });
                                    });
                            
                                    function updateReactionCounts(reactionCounts) {
                                        for (const [reactionType, count] of Object.entries(reactionCounts)) {
                                            const countElement = document.getElementById(`${reactionType}-count`);
                                            if (countElement) {
                                                countElement.textContent = count; 
                                            }
                                        }
                            
                                        const totalResponsesElement = document.getElementById("total-responses");
                                        if (totalResponsesElement) {
                                            const totalResponses = Object.values(reactionCounts).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
                                            totalResponsesElement.textContent = totalResponses;
                                        }
                                    }
                                });
                            
                            </script>                        </div>

<script>
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
        var listItemsPremium = document.querySelectorAll("#premium .list-group-item");
        var showMoreBtnPremium = document.getElementById("show-more-btn-premium");

        var listItemsPaid = document.querySelectorAll("#paid .list-group-item");
        var showMoreBtnPaid = document.getElementById("show-more-btn-paid");

        var listItemsPlanitum = document.querySelectorAll("#platinum .list-group-item");
        var showMoreBtnPlatinum = document.getElementById("show-more-btn-platinum");


        var maxVisible = 6;

        if (listItemsPremium.length > maxVisible) {
            for (var i = maxVisible; i < listItemsPremium.length; i++) {
                listItemsPremium[i].style.display = "none";
            }
            showMoreBtnPremium.style.display = "block"; 
        }

        if (listItemsPlanitum.length > maxVisible) {
            for (var i = maxVisible; i < listItemsPlanitum.length; i++) {
                listItemsPlanitum[i].style.display = "none";
            }
            showMoreBtnPlatinum.style.display = "block"; 
        }


        if (listItemsPaid.length > maxVisible) {
            for (var i = maxVisible; i < listItemsPaid.length; i++) {
                listItemsPaid[i].style.display = "none";
            }
            showMoreBtnPaid.style.display = "block"; 
        }



        if (showMoreBtnPaid) {
            showMoreBtnPaid.addEventListener("click", function () {
                for (var i = maxVisible; i < listItemsPaid.length; i++) {
                    listItemsPaid[i].style.display = "block";
                }
                showMoreBtnPaid.style.display = "none"; 
            });
        }


        if (showMoreBtnPremium) {
            showMoreBtnPremium.addEventListener("click", function () {
                for (var i = maxVisible; i < listItemsPremium.length; i++) {
                    listItemsPremium[i].style.display = "block";
                }
                showMoreBtnPremium.style.display = "none"; 
            });
        }

        if (showMoreBtnPlatinum) {
            showMoreBtnPlatinum.addEventListener("click", function () {
                for (var i = maxVisible; i < listItemsPlanitum.length; i++) {
                    listItemsPlanitum[i].style.display = "block";
                }
                showMoreBtnPlatinum.style.display = "none"; 
            });

        }
    });
</script>

        function getChapterStyle() {
            var a = $.cookie("chapter_style");
            return (a = a ? JSON.parse(a) : {}).background || (a.background = "#F4F4F4"), a.fontFamily || (a.fontFamily = "Arial, sans-serif"), a.fontSize || (a.fontSize = "18px"), a.lineHeight || (a.lineHeight = "160%"), a.fluidSwitch || (a.fluidSwitch = "no"), a.onebreakSwitch || (a.onebreakSwitch = "no"), a.navBar || (a.navBar = "close"), a
        }
        const chapter_style = getChapterStyle();

        const toggleButton = document.getElementById('toggle-dark-mode');
        const container = document.getElementById('container');
        const $footerDark = $("footer");

        if(chapter_style && chapter_style.background && chapter_style.background =='#232323') {
            container.classList.add('dark-background');
            $footerDark.addClass("footer-dark");
            toggleButton.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-moon"></i>'; 
        } else {
            container.classList.remove('dark-background');
            $footerDark.removeClass("footer-dark");
            toggleButton.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-sun"></i>'; 
        }

        toggleButton.addEventListener('click', function () {

            if (container.classList.contains('dark-background')) {
                container.classList.remove('dark-background');

                toggleButton.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-sun"></i>'; // Light mode icon
                chapter_style.background = '#F4F4F4';
                container.removeAttribute('style');
                container.setAttribute('style', 'background-color: #F4F4F4;');
                $footerDark.removeClass("footer-dark");

            } else {
                container.classList.add('dark-background');
                container.removeAttribute('style');
                toggleButton.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-moon"></i>'; // Dark mode icon
                chapter_style.background = '#232323';
                $footerDark.addClass("footer-dark");
            }
            var n = new Date;
            n.setTime(n.getTime() + 6048e5),
                $.cookie("chapter_style", JSON.stringify(chapter_style), { path: "/", expires: n });

        });
